Because the robot delivered the meal to the door of the room, the child took the room card out to get the meal and accidentally dropped the room card on the corridor. It was really spooky and I didn‚Äôt know where it went.
I couldn‚Äôt get in, so I asked the waiter for an extra room card and was told to compensate 30 yuan. This really surprised me. As a listed five-star hotel standard, it costs 30 yuan to get an extra room card. The waiter said that if they didn‚Äôt charge 30 yuan, they would have to pay 30 yuan themselves.
I have stayed in other five-star hotels around the world for decades, and the hotel has never argued with guests about paying 30 yuan for missing room cards. If you want one or two more, you can give it at will, and it‚Äôs okay if you accidentally take it away. Home Inn has never asked guests to pay 30 yuan for room cards.

Shanwei Wyndham Hotel is really a hotel management standard thinking of the 1980s, and if you don‚Äôt see it, you will lose money.

I never write bad reviews for hotels I've stayed in, but after thinking for a long time, I decided to write down the true experience. First, I'm a local, and I hope my hometown can become more civilized and progressive, and have a good five-star hotel. Second, I don't want the backward service thinking of this Wyndham Hotel to have a negative impact on foreign guests, and don't slap the face of Haifeng people.

I hope the owner of this hotel can see my message, and can develop a big business in Haifeng, and don't care about small money anymore.

Objectively speaking, Wyndham Xiamen is really great. The staff are polite and proactive. The service attitude is not even as good as the homestays in Nan'ao Island, Shantou. If you don't raise awareness and broaden your horizons, it will only drag down the brand.
